                                 (a)->y > (b)->y ? ((r)->y = (a)->y) \
                                                 : ((r)->y = (b)->y),\
                                 (a)->z > (b)->z ? ((r)->z = (a)->z) \
                                                 : ((r)->z = (b)->z))
\end{verbatim}\normalsize

{\bf Value:}

\footnotesize\begin{verbatim}((a)->x < (b)->x ? ((r)->x = (a)->x) \
                                                 : ((r)->x = (b)->x),\
                                 (a)->y < (b)->y ? ((r)->y = (a)->y) \
                                                 : ((r)->y = (b)->y),\
                                 (a)->z < (b)->z ? ((r)->z = (a)->z) \
                                                 : ((r)->z = (b)->z))
\end{verbatim}\normalsize
